beginSubroutine: s32'CheckVoiceFunc'
  returnValue: 0, 0
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(0)
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'bgt'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      returnValue: 0, 1
    endIf: 
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'sin'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      returnValue: 0, 1
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(1)
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'bgt'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      returnValue: 0, 1
    endIf: 
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'sin'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      returnValue: 0, 1
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'bgt'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      returnValue: 0, 1
    endIf: 
    ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'sin'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      returnValue: 0, 1
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_Dust_HomingJump'
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(0)
    setEventTrigger: (TIMER), 78
    upon: (TIMER)
      upon: (IDLING)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(50)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000)
        endIf: 
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
          ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
            spriteBlend: s32'sol035_01', 2, 45
          endIf: 
          else: 
            spriteBlend: s32'sol035_02', 2, 45
            ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
              storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
            endIf: 
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon:

    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg12), Val(0)

    groundHitEffect: (AIR_FACE_UP)
    airHitEffect: (AIR_FACE_UP)
    hitAirPushbackX: 0, 2000
    hitAirPushbackY: 0, 45000
    landingAutoAction: 0
    upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'landing'
    endUpon: 
    haltMomentum: 0
    upon: (HIT_OR_GUARD)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (HIT_OR_GUARD)
      extendPushboxX: 100000
      callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmn_screenshake', Val(3), Val(2), Val(0), Val(0)
    endUpon: 
    upon: (HIT)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (HIT)
      checkMoveFlag: (ENEMY_AIRBORNE)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyPushDistance), Val(250000)
          ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDistanceY), Val(90000)
            ifNot: Mem(IsEnemyPlayerDown)
              storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        if: Mem(IsEnemyDamage)
          ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyPushDistance), Val(140000)
            ifNot: Mem(IsEnemyPlayerDown)
              storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
        else: 
          ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyPushDistance), Val(30000)
            ifNot: Mem(IsEnemyPlayerDown)
              storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endElse: 
      endElse: 
    endUpon: 
    callSubroutine: s32'BeginingMoveCheck'
    wallBlowoffType: 2
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaActReg0), Val(-200000)
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaActReg1), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaActReg2), Val(0)
    hitSoundEffect: s32'SE_BTL_CMN_Hit_Grap_L'
    guardSoundEffect: s32'SE_BTL_CMN_Guard_Grap_L'
    spriteSlowParam: 1, 1, 6, 100, 60, 300
    spriteSlowParamFinishStop: 1, 1, 6, 100, 200, 300
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_wildassault_Inertia'
  endUpon:

  callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmnAddTensionGG', Val(1), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
